Profile





 Profile





Profile










                                Dr. Barsha Mitra


 Assistant Professor Department of Computer Science & Information Systems BITS Pilani, Hyderabad Campus Educational Background  1. Doctor of Philosophy, Department of Computer Science & Engineering, Indian Institute of Technology Kharagpur, 2016. 2. Master of Engineering, Information Technology, Jadavpur University, 2011. 3. Bachelor of Technology, Information Technology, West Bengal University of Technology, 2009.  Contact Details: Room No. B 203,Dept. of  Computer Science & Information System,BITS Pilani, Hyderabad Campus,Jawahar Nagar, Kapra Mandal,Medchal District,Secunderabad - 500078,Telangana State Email: barsha.mitra@hyderabad.bits-pilani.ac.in

Profile





 Profile





Profile










                                Dr. Barsha Mitra


 Assistant Professor Department of Computer Science & Information Systems BITS Pilani, Hyderabad Campus Educational Background  1. Doctor of Philosophy, Department of Computer Science & Engineering, Indian Institute of Technology Kharagpur, 2016. 2. Master of Engineering, Information Technology, Jadavpur University, 2011. 3. Bachelor of Technology, Information Technology, West Bengal University of Technology, 2009.  Contact Details: Room No. B 203,Dept. of  Computer Science & Information System,BITS Pilani, Hyderabad Campus,Jawahar Nagar, Kapra Mandal,Medchal District,Secunderabad - 500078,Telangana State Email: barsha.mitra@hyderabad.bits-pilani.ac.in
